NOTE: New Caledonia, Fiji and Vanuatu advance to Oceania second round,
      a four-country OFC Nations Cup tournament with New Zealand. The
      OFC Nations Cup champion plays an Asian Football Confederation
      (AFC) team in a two-match series, with winner advancing to the
      2010 World Cup in South Africa.
